Events — Interface event index

Generated from Interface/ in interface.zip. Build time: 2026-02-13 21:57:10.

How this page was built

  • Registered pointers come from string-literal calls such as :RegisterEvent("EVENT"), :RegisterEvents("A,B"), :RegisterEvents(('A', 'B')), and simple C_Hook:Register(...) usages.
  • Handled pointers come from literal comparisons like if event == "EVENT" then (including elseif chains).
  • If an event shows “no explicit registration/handling”, it may still exist via variables, loop registration, XML-embedded scripts, or native code.

Counts: 807 total events found; 734 with explicit registration sites; 640 with explicit handler checks.
